		CombosArray[1270-1][0] = "Zimmer";CombosArray[1270-1][1] = "Golden_Spirit";
	
		CombosArray[1271-1][0] = "Zimmer";CombosArray[1271-1][1] = "Quicksilver";
	


function clearModels()
	{
	var optionCount = document.advancedForm.Model.length;
	for (i=optionCount-1; i>0; i--)
		{
		document.advancedForm.Model.options[i] = null;
		}
	}


// Add in the Models which belong to the chosen Make.	
function changeModels()
	{
	var optionCtr = 1;
	clearModels();
	if (document.advancedForm.Make.selectedIndex == 0)
		{document.advancedForm.Model.options[0] = new Option("Select Make Above", "");
		document.advancedForm.Model.disabled = true;}
	else
		{document.advancedForm.Model.options[0] = new Option("Please Choose Model", "");
		document.advancedForm.Model.disabled = false;}
		
	for (i=0; i<CombosArray.length; i++)
		{
		// Yes, we need the parseInt function, otherwise Netscape can't figure out when the numbers are equal.
		if(document.advancedForm.Make.options[document.advancedForm.Make.selectedIndex].value == CombosArray[i][0])
			{
			newModel = new Option(CombosArray[i][1].replace(/_/g, ' '), CombosArray[i][1], false, false)
			document.advancedForm.Model.options[optionCtr] = newModel;
			optionCtr ++;
			}
		}
	
	// Reset menu to the first choice for lame Netscape browsers.
	document.advancedForm.Model.selectedIndex = 0;
	}

// -->

	function HighlightCell(CellInteger, CellIDNumber)
		{
		for (i=1;i<=iNumberOfCells;i++)
			{
			if (i != CellIDNumber)
				{
				document.getElementById(CellInteger + '_' + i).className = 'ResultsLinkOn';

	function UnHighlightCell(CellInteger)

	function doAdvancedSearch(theform)
		{
		if (theform.Year1.value == '' && theform.Make.value == '' && theform.Model.value == '')
			{
			window.location.href = '/Vehicles/NewListings.cfm';
			return false;
			}
		else
			{
			return true;
			}
		}
	function doQuickSearch(theform)
		{
		if (trim(theform.SearchText.value) == '' && theform.zip.value.length < 5)
			{
			window.location.href = '/Vehicles/NewListings.cfm';
			return false;
			}
		else if (theform.zip.value.length < 5) //use the new urlRewriter format
			{
			s = theform.SearchText.value;
			s = trim(s);
			s = s.replace(/ /g,'_');
			window.location.href='/used_cars_for_sale/'+s;
			return false;
			}
		else //submit as normal
			{
			return true;
			}
		}
	
	function tabs_action(id,action)
		{
		if (action == 'over')
			{
			if (id != tabs_curTab)
				{document.getElementById('tab_'+id).src = '/Images/Homepage_Tabs/'+tabs_style+'/'+id+'_Over.jpg';}
			}
		if (action == 'out')
			{
			if (id != tabs_curTab)
				{document.getElementById('tab_'+id).src = '/Images/Homepage_Tabs/'+tabs_style+'/'+id+'_Off.jpg';}
			}
		if (action == 'click')
			{
			if (id != tabs_curTab)
				{
				document.getElementById('tab_'+id).src = '/Images/Homepage_Tabs/'+tabs_style+'/'+id+'_On.jpg';
				document.getElementById('tab_'+tabs_curTab).src = '/Images/Homepage_Tabs/'+tabs_style+'/'+tabs_curTab+'_Off.jpg';
				
				//fade out the current, and fade in the new
				document.getElementById('tab_'+id+'_div').style.display = '';
				opacity('tab_'+id+'_div',0,100,100);
				opacity('tab_'+tabs_curTab+'_div',100,0,200);
				setTimeout("document.getElementById('tab_"+tabs_curTab+"_div').style.display = 'none';",201);
				
				tabs_curTab = id;
				}
			}
		}
	
	function tabs_rotate()
		{
		tabs_curTabNum ++;
		if (tabs_curTabNum > 3)
			tabs_curTabNum = 1;
			
		if (tabs_curTabNum == 1)
			tabs_action('MostViewed','click');
		if (tabs_curTabNum == 2)
			tabs_action('NewestListings','click');
		if (tabs_curTabNum == 3)
			tabs_action('Spotlight','click');
		}
